					<div class="elementor-shortcode"><div class="menu-container" onclick="menuAnimation(this)">
  <div class="bar1"></div>
  <div class="bar2"></div>
  <div class="bar3"></div>
</div>
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
    $('.rk-menu').hide();
  });
  jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
      if(localStorage.getItem("menuActive") === 'true'){
        $('.rk-menu').fadeToggle();
        $('.menu-container').addClass('change')
      }
    });
  
function menuAnimation(x) {
  jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
      if($('.menu-container').hasClass('change')){
    localStorage.setItem("menuActive", false);
    $('.rk-menu').hide();
    $('.menu-container').removeClass('change')
 }else{
    localStorage.setItem("menuActive", true);
    $('.rk-menu').fadeToggle();
    x.classList.toggle("change");
 }
  });
  
  
}
</script></div>

				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="elementor-shortcode"><div class="menu-container" onclick="menuAnimation(this)">
  <div class="bar1"></div>
  <div class="bar2"></div>
  <div class="bar3"></div>
</div>
<script>
jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
    $('.rk-menu').hide();
  });
  jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
      if(localStorage.getItem("menuActive") === 'true'){
        $('.rk-menu').fadeToggle();
        $('.menu-container').addClass('change')
      }
    });
  
function menuAnimation(x) {
  jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
      if($('.menu-container').hasClass('change')){
    localStorage.setItem("menuActive", false);
    $('.rk-menu').hide();
    $('.menu-container').removeClass('change')
 }else{
    localStorage.setItem("menuActive", true);
    $('.rk-menu').fadeToggle();
    x.classList.toggle("change");
 }
  });
  
  
}
</script></div>
